INTERPRETATION
----------------------------------------
AT-RISK tables have mean_rows variables where sum(!is.na(var)) < nrow(data).
If a NET row is created from these components, the current R code would use
the first component's non-NA count as the base instead of the full table base.
This produces wrong base numbers (the S9/Tito's bug).
